2025-01-24T14:30:01.3269600Z   The behavior will change in pandas 3.0. This inplace method will never work because the intermediate object on which we are setting values always behaves as a copy.
2025-01-24T14:30:01.3269650Z   
2025-01-24T14:30:01.3270060Z   For example, when doing 'df[col].method(value, inplace=True)', try using 'df.method({col: value}, inplace=True)' or df[col] = df[col].method(value) instead, to perform the operation inplace on the original object.
